                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }
                      </script>

                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }
                      </script>

                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       decorateGeneric($$('ul.products-grid'), ['odd', 'even', 'first', 'last'])
                      </script>
                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;

                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      decorateGeneric($$('ul.products-grid'), ['odd', 'even', 'first', 'last'])
                     </script>
                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;

                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }
