                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                     <script type="text/javascript">
                      if (!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         function widthCorrector() {
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-7549');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth / widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth / columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-7549 .widget-slider li.item{width:' + columnWidth + 'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
 
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                             widthCorrector()
                         });
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function () {
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_7549() {
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .products-grid li.item').each(function () {
                                 if (jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height) {
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-7549 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
 
                     widget_slider_height_7549();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function () {
                         widget_slider_height_7549();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
 
                     function resizer() {
 //                        if(resflag == true){
 //                            resflag = false;
 //                            setTimeout(function(){
 //                                jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
 //                                setTimeout(function(){
 //                                    resflag = true;
 //                                }, 500);
 //                            }, 1000);
 //                        }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function () {
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function () {
                         if (!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')) {
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick: true,
                             width: 600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type: 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function () {
                                 setTimeout(function () {
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if (jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight + 30) {
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
 
                 function showOptions(url) {
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
 
                 function setAjaxData1(data, iframe, name, image) {
                     if (data.status == 'ERROR') {
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message + '<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     } else {
                         if (data.sidebar) {
                             if (jQuery('.top-cart')) {
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if (jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length) {
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         } else {
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function (html) {
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function (event) {
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('href') + '" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function () {
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         setTimeout(function () {
                                             window.location.reload();
                                         }, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src=' + image + ' alt=""></span><span>' + name + '</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)
                     }, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function () {
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
 
                 function setLocationAjax1(url, id, name, image) {
                     console.log('set location ajax function activated on slider-owl');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart", "ajax/index");
 //                    var selectorr = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).show();
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader' + id;
 //                    console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display': 'block'});
                     jQuery(selectorId).show();
 //                    console.log('simple'+ jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).length);
 //                    console.log('constructed' +jQuery(selectorId).length);
 //                    jQuery('.ajax_loader-item').show();
 
                     jQuery("#header .owl-carousel .button-holder").on('click', function () {
 //                        console.log('clicked');
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").length);
 //                        console.log(jQuery(".ajax-loader-item", this).length);
                         jQuery(this).find(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'block'});
                         jQuery(selectorId).show();
                     });
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url: url,
                             dataType: 'json',
                             success: function (data) {
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader' + id).hide();
                                 jQuery(".ajax-loader-item").css({'display': 'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData1(data, false, name, image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
                         console.log('cannot add to cart slider owl');
                     }
                 }

                 jQuery("#login-holder").addClass('show');
 
 
             });

                 jQuery("#login-holder").removeClass('show');
                 jQuery("#login-holder").addClass('hide');
 
                 jQuery("#login-holder-small").removeClass('show');
                 jQuery("#login-holder-small").addClass('hide');
             });
 
 
 //            jQuery('.top-link-login.big').hover(

             jQuery('.top-link-login').on('click', function (e) {
                 e.preventDefault();
 
                 if (jQuery(".login-holder").hasClass('show')) {
                     jQuery(".login-holder").removeClass('show');
                     jQuery(".login-holder").addClass('hide');
                 } else {
                     jQuery(".login-holder").removeClass('hide');
                     jQuery(".login-holder").addClass('show');
 
                 }
             });

   <script>
    (function () {
         var isBootstrapEvent = false;
         if (window.jQuery) {
             var all = jQuery('*');
             jQuery.each(['hide.bs.dropdown',
                 'hide.bs.collapse',
                 'hide.bs.modal',
                 'hide.bs.tooltip',
                 'hide.bs.bstooltip',
                 'hide.bs.popover',
                 'hide.bs.tab'], function (index, eventName) {
                 all.on(eventName, function (event) {
                     isBootstrapEvent = true;
                 });
             });
         }
         var originalHide = Element.hide;
         Element.addMethods({
             hide: function (element) {
                 if (isBootstrapEvent) {
                     isBootstrapEvent = false;
                     return element;
                 }
                 return originalHide(element);
             }
         });
     })();
   </script>

           <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-9 col-md-offset-3 col-lg-9 col-lg-offset-3" id="maimuta_form">

                </i>

               <div id="popup-form-content">
                <h2 style="margin-top:0;font-family: 'Bungee';color:#da251d;font-size: 24px;">
                 Bine ai venit la Bebelusultau.ro
                </h2>
                <div id="popup-text">

           <script type="text/javascript">
            var form = jQuery('.popup-form-data');
         var container = jQuery('#maimuta_form');
         var email = jQuery("#email");
         var email_error_msg = jQuery('#email_error_msg');
 
         function emailCookieExists() {
             if (Mage.Cookies.get('email')) {
                 return true
             }
             else {
                 return false
             }
         }
 
         function checkShowCookie() {
             var cookieCheck = Mage.Cookies.get('formShow');
             var abortCheck = Mage.Cookies.get('counter');
             if (abortCheck) {
                 container.remove();
                 console.log('said no, not showing');
             } else {
                 console.log('no nope cookie');
                 var shownLimit = 1;
                 if (!cookieCheck) {
                     console.log('cookie not found, setting');
 
                     createCookie('formShow', 1, '1');
                     track('event','CustomPopIn','Shown','CustomPopIn Shown');
                 } else {
                     var newValue = ++cookieCheck;
                     console.log(newValue);
                     if (cookieCheck <= shownLimit) {
                         createCookie('formShow', newValue, 1);
                     }
                     if (cookieCheck > shownLimit) {
                         console.log('reached ShownLimit, removing');
                         track('event','CustomPopIn','ShownLimitReached','CustomPopIn ShownLimitReached');
                         container.remove();
                     }
                 }
             }
         }
 
         checkShowCookie();
         if (!emailCookieExists()) {
             jQuery(email).show();
             jQuery(form).show();
             jQuery(container).show();
         } else {
             jQuery(container).hide();
         }
 
         function validateEmail(email) {
             var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
             return re.test(email);
         }
 
         function createCookie(name, value, expirationInDays) {
             var now = new Date();
             var expire = new Date(now.getTime() + (expirationInDays * 24 * 60) * 60000);//[(1 * 365 * 24 * 60) * 60000] == 1 year  -- (Years * Days * Hours * Minutes) * 60000
             //document.cookie = cookie + '; expires=' + expire + '; path=/';
             Mage.Cookies.expires = expire;
             Mage.Cookies.set(name, value);
         }
 
         function readCookie(name) {
             var nameEQ = name + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                 if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
             }
             return null;
         }
 
         function abort() {
             container.hide();
             track('event','CustomPopIn','Closed','CustomPopIn Closed');
                         createCookie('email', 'none', "30");
                                 }
 
         function sendForm() {
             console.log(form);
             var inputFieldEmail = $$('.email_input input[type=text]').first();
             var inputFieldFName = $$('.fname_input input[type=text]').first();
             var inputFieldLName = $$('.lname_input input[type=text]').first();
             var email = inputFieldEmail.value;
             var fname = '';
             var lname = '';
             if (inputFieldFName) {
                 fname = inputFieldFName.value;
             }
             if (inputFieldLName) {
                 lname = inputFieldLName.value;
             }
             track('event','CustomPopIn','Subscribe','CustomPopIn Subscribed');
             if (validateEmail(email)) {
                 createCookie('email', email + '/' + fname + '/' + lname, 365);
                 console.log(email);
 
                                 createCookie('subscribe', 'true', 365);
                 location.reload();
                             } else {
 
                 jQuery(email_error_msg).text('Adresa de mail introdusa nu este valida');
                 jQuery(email_error_msg).css('color', 'red');
                 email_error_msg.show();
             }
         }
 
         function track(event, Category, Action, Label){
             ga('send',{
                 hitType: event,
                 eventCategory: Category,
                 eventAction: Action,
                 label: Label
             });
             console.log(event,Category,Action,Label);
         }
           </script>
          </div>

               <script type="text/javascript">
                jQuery(document).ready(function(){
 			jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
 				{
 				   hideOnContentClick : true,
 				   width:600,
 				   autoDimensions: true,
 				   type : 'iframe',
 				   showTitle: false,
 				   scrolling: 'no',
 				   afterLoad: function(){
 						setTimeout(function(){
 							var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
 							if(jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight+30){
 								jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
 							}
 						}, 1000);
 					}
 				}
 			);
 			
 					});
 		function showOptions(url){
 			jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
 			jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
 			setTimeout(function(){
 				jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
 			}, 1000);
 		}
 		function setAjaxData(data,iframe,name,image){
 			if(data.status == 'ERROR'){
 				jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message+'<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
 			}else{
 				if(data.sidebar){
 					if(jQuery('.top-cart')){
 						jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
 						if(jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length){
 							jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
 						}
 					}
 					jQuery.fancybox.close();
                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="product-image"><img src='+ image+' alt=""></span>' + name +'<a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 					
 				}else{
 					jQuery.ajax({
 						url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
 						cache: false
 					}).done(function(html){
 						jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
 						jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function(event){
 							event.preventDefault();
 							jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="'+ jQuery(this).attr('href') +'" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
 							jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function(){
 								link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
 								jQuery.ajax({
 									url: link,
 									cache: false
 								});
 								jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
 								setTimeout(function(){window.location.reload();}, 800);
 							});
 						});
 					});
 					jQuery.fancybox.close();
                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="product-image"><img src='+ image+' alt=""></span>' + name +'<a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 				}
 			}
 			setTimeout(function () {jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)}, 5000);
 			jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function(){
 				jQuery(this).parent().slideUp(500);
 				return false;
 			});
 		}
 		function setLocationAjax(url,id,name,image){
 			url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
 			url = url.replace("checkout/cart","ajax/index");
 			jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).show();
 			try {
 				jQuery.ajax({
 					url : url,
 					dataType : 'json',
 					success : function(data) {
 						jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).hide();
 						jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
 						setAjaxData(data,false,name,image);
 					}
 				});
 			} catch (e) {
 			}
 		}
               </script>
              </div>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               jQuery(window).load(function(){
 			jQuery('brands.slider-container').each(function(){
 				if(!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')){
 					jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
 				}
 			});
 			function sliderLauncher3506(){
 				jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .widget-slider').iosSlider({
 					responsiveSlideWidth: true,
 					snapToChildren: true,
 					desktopClickDrag: true,
 					infiniteSlider: false
 					,
 										navNextSelector: '#brand-slider-3506 .next',
 					navPrevSelector: '#brand-slider-3506 .prev'
 									});
 			}
 			function brands_slider_height_3506(){
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					var brands_slider_height = 0;
 					jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .brands li').each(function(){
 						if(jQuery(this).height() > brands_slider_height){
 							brands_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
 						}
 					})
 					jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .widget-slider').css({
 						'min-height': (brands_slider_height+2),
 						'height': 'auto'
 					});
 					
 				}, 1000);
 			}
 			brands_slider_height_3506();
 			jQuery(window).resize(function(){
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .widget-slider').iosSlider('update');
 				}, 500);
 				brands_slider_height_3506();
 			});
 			
 			/* Slider Start */
 			slidesWidth = 0;
 			jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .brands li').each(function(){
 				slidesWidth += jQuery(this).outerWidth(true);
 			});
 			
 			if(slidesWidth > 1252){
 				sliderLauncher3506();
 			}else{
 				jQuery('#brand-slider-3506').addClass('slider-off');
 			}
 			
 			jQuery(window).on('orientationchange', function(e){
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					jQuery('#brand-slider-3506 .widget-slider').iosSlider('update');
 				}, 500);
 			});
 		 });
              </script>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

                decorateGeneric($$('ul.products-grid'), ['odd','even','first','last'])

               <script type="text/javascript">
                if(!jQuery('body').hasClass('mobile-device')){
                     setTimeout(function(){
                         function widthCorrector(){
                             var widget = jQuery('#home-slider-6076');
                             widget.children('style').remove();
                             var widgetWidth = widget.width();
                             //widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').attr('style', '');
                             var widgetItemWidth = widget.find('.widget-slider li.item:first').width();
                             setTimeout(function(){
                                 var columnsCount = Math.round(widgetWidth/widgetItemWidth);
                                 var columnWidth = Math.floor(widgetWidth/columnsCount);
                                 var widgetItemsCss = '<style type="text/css">#home-slider-6076 .widget-slider li.item{width:'+ columnWidth +'px;}</style>';
                                 widget.append(widgetItemsCss);
                             }, 300);
                         }
                         widthCorrector();
                         jQuery(window).resize(function(){widthCorrector()});
                     }, 300);
                 }
                 
                 jQuery(window).load(function(){
                     
                     function widget_slider_height_6076(){
                         setTimeout(function(){
                             var widget_slider_height = 0;
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-6076 .products-grid li.item').each(function(){
                                 if(jQuery(this).height() > widget_slider_height){
                                     widget_slider_height = jQuery(this).height();
                                 }
                             })
                             jQuery('.widget-container #home-slider-6076 .widget-slider').css({
 //                                'min-height': (widget_slider_height+2),
                                 'height': 'auto'
                             });
 
                         }, 1000);
                     }
                     widget_slider_height_6076();
 
                     jQuery(window).resize(function(){
                         widget_slider_height_6076();
                         resizer();
                     });
                     var resflag = true;
                     function resizer(){
                         if(resflag == true){
                             resflag = false;
                             setTimeout(function(){
                                 jQuery(window).trigger('resize');
                                 setTimeout(function(){
                                     resflag = true;
                                 }, 500);
                             }, 1000);
                         }
                     }
                 });
                 
 
                 jQuery(document).ready(function(){
                     jQuery('.widget-container').each(function(){
                         if(!jQuery(this).prev().hasClass('page-title')){
                             jQuery(this).addClass('no-title');
                         }
                     });
 
                     jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
                         {
                             hideOnContentClick : true,
                             width:600,
                             autoDimensions: true,
                             type : 'iframe',
                             showTitle: false,
                             scrolling: 'no',
                             afterLoad: function(){
                                 setTimeout(function(){
                                     var frameBodyHeight = jQuery('.fancybox-iframe').contents().find('body').height();
                                     if(jQuery(window).height() > frameBodyHeight+30){
                                         jQuery('.fancybox-inner').css('height', frameBodyHeight);
                                     }
                                 }, 1000);
                             }
                         }
                     );
 
                                     });
                 function showOptions(url){
                     jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', url);
                     jQuery('#fancybox').trigger('click');
                     setTimeout(function(){
                         jQuery('#fancybox').attr('href', '#');
                     }, 1000);
                 }
                 function setAjaxData(data,iframe,name,image){
                     if(data.status == 'ERROR'){
                         console.log('could not set ajax data owl 666666');
                         jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success">' + data.message+'<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times" /></a></div>');
                     }else{
                         if(data.sidebar){
                             if(jQuery('.top-cart')){
                                 jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
                                 if(jQuery('#cart-sidebar').length){
                                     jQuery('#cart-sidebar').html(jQuery(data.sidebar).find('#mini-cart'));
                                 }
                             }
                             jQuery('#cart-items-count').html(data.items);
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src='+ image+' alt=""></span><span>' + name +'</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
 
                         }else{
                             jQuery.ajax({
                                 url: "https://bebelusultau.ro/incognitoactions/updatecart/?isAjax=true/",
                                 cache: false
                             }).done(function(html){
                                 jQuery('header#header .top-cart').replaceWith(html);
                                 jQuery('.top-cart #mini-cart li.item a.btn-remove').on('click', function(event){
                                     event.preventDefault();
                                     jQuery('body').append('<div class="cart-remove-box">Esti sigur ca vrei sa stergi produsul din cos?<br/><a href="'+ jQuery(this).attr('href') +'" class="confirm"><span>Ok</span></a><a href="#" class="cancel"><span>Anuleaza</span></a></div>');
                                     jQuery('.cart-remove-box a').on('click', function(){
                                         link = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                                         jQuery.ajax({
                                             url: link,
                                             cache: false
                                         });
                                         jQuery('.cart-remove-box').remove();
                                         //setTimeout(function(){window.location.reload();}, 800);
                                     });
                                 });
                             });
                             jQuery.fancybox.close();
                             jQuery('body').append('<div class="add-to-cart-success"><p>Produsul a fost adaugat in cos<a href="#" class="btn-remove"><i class="fa fa-times"></i></a></p><span class="meta"><span class="product-image"><img src='+ image+' alt=""></span><span>' + name +'</span></span><a class="button" href="https://bebelusultau.ro/checkout/cart/"><span>Vezi Detalii Cos</span></a></div>');
                         }
                     }
                     setTimeout(function () {jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500)}, 5000);
                     jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function(){
                         jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
                         return false;
                     });
                 }
                 function setLocationAjax(url,id,name,image){
                     console.log('set location ajax activated owl 666');
                     url += 'isAjax/1?isAjax=true';
                     url = url.replace("checkout/cart","ajax/index");
                     var selectorId = '#ajax_loader'+id;
                     console.log(selectorId);
                     jQuery(selectorId).css({'display':'block'});
 //                    jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).show();
                     try {
                         jQuery.ajax({
                             url : url,
                             dataType : 'json',
                             success : function(data) {
 //                                console.log('success add to cart owl 666');
                                 console.log(data);
                                 jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).css({'display':'none'});
                                 jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
                                 setAjaxData(data,false,name,image);
                             }
                         });
                     } catch (e) {
 //                        console.log('cannot add to cart owl 6');
                     }
                 }
               </script>

                     Politica de confidențialitate
                    </a>
                    si accept sa primesc comunicări comerciale personalizate de la Bebelusultau.ro prin email sau prin alte mijloace.

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 jQuery('.block-subscribe button.button').on('click', function(){
 		jQuery('#firstname, #lastname').each(function(){
 			if(jQuery(this).attr('data-placeholder') == jQuery(this).attr('value')){
 				jQuery(this).attr('value', '');
 			}
 		});
 		setTimeout(function(){
 			if(jQuery('#newsletter_402').hasClass('validation-failed') ){
 				jQuery('#firstname, #lastname').each(function(){
 					if(jQuery(this).attr('value') == ''){
 						jQuery(this).attr('value', jQuery(this).attr('data-placeholder'));
 					}
 				});
 			}
 			
 		}, 10);
 				setTimeout(function(){
 			jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice').removeClass('active').attr('style', '');
 			if(jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice').length > 1){
 				if(jQuery('#newsletter_402').attr('value') == ''){
 					jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice').first().addClass('active');
 				}else{
 					jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice').eq(1).addClass('active');
 				}
 			}else{
 				jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice').addClass('active');
 			}
 			activeMsg = jQuery('#popup-block .input-box .validation-advice.active');
 			if(parseFloat(activeMsg.css('min-height')) < activeMsg.height()){
 				activeMsg.css('bottom', '-'+activeMsg.height()+'px');
 			}
 		}, 1200);
 			});
     //<![CDATA[
         var newsletterSubscriberFormDetail = new VarienForm('newsletter-validate-detail_402');
     //]]>
 	if(jQuery('.block-subscribe').parents('#popup-block').length) {
 		jQuery('#popup-block .block-subscribe .actions button.button').on('click', function(){
 			var button = jQuery(this);
 			setTimeout(function(){
 				if(!button.parent().find('input#newsletter_402').hasClass('validation-failed')){
 					jQuery.cookie('incognitoPopupFlag', 'true', {
 						path: '/'
 					});
 				}
 			}, 500);
 		});
 	}
                </script>
